---
layout: "post"
title: "HoTT-Book Exercises"
date: "2018-04-08"
categories: type-theory
---

This is a self-contained version of some solutions for HoTT-Book's exercises.
The idea is to unpackage all as long as possible to get a better understanding.
Many changes can be appear running this experiment. The solutions are
type-checked as a whole using Agda v2.5.3.


## Requirements

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An Agda pragma for consistency with HoTT:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="524" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="528" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="536" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="548" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Equality type defintion also called Identity type:

## Chapter 1

### Exercise 1.1

<div class="exercise">
Given functions $$f : A \to B$$ and $$g:B\to C$$, define
their composite $$ g\circ f:A\to C$$.
</div>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_∘_" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%88%98_" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a> <a id="1997" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1999" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2001" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2002" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2002" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="2004" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2004" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="2006" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2006" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2007" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2009" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2010" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2010" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2012" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2014" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2018" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2002" class="Bound">i</a><a id="2019" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2021" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2021" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2023" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2025" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2029" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2004" class="Bound">j</a><a id="2030" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2032" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2032" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="2034" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2036" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2040" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2006" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2041" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="2047" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2049" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2050" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2021" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2052" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2054" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2032" class="Bound">C</a><a id="2055" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="2061" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2063" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2064" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2010" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2066" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2068" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2021" class="Bound">B</a><a id="2069" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="2075" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2077" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2010" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2079" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2081" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2032" class="Bound">C</a>
<a id="2083" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2083" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2085" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%88%98_" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="2087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2087" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2089" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2091" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="2093" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2093" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2095" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2097" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2083" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2099" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2100" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2087" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2102" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#2093" class="Bound">x</a><a id="2103" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
<div class="exercise">
Show that we have $$h \circ (g\circ f) \equiv (h\circ g)\circ f$$.
</div>
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="∘-assoc" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%E2%88%98-assoc" class="Function">∘-assoc</a> <a id="2234" class="Symbol">:</a> <a ### Exercise 1.2

<div class="exercise">
Derive the recursion principle for products $$\mathsf{rec}_{A\times B}$$
using only the projections, and verify that the definitional equalities
are valid. Do the same for $$\Sigma$$-types.
</div>

Let's add some machinery to handle levels of the universe needed for
the following exercises including this one:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2772" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="2777" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="2784" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="2799" class="Keyword">public</a>
  <a id="2808" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="2814" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2815" href="Agda.Primitive.html#Level" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="2820" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="2822" href="Agda.Primitive.html#_%E2%8A%94_" class="Primitive Operator">_⊔_</a><a id="2825" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="2827" href="Agda.Primitive.html#lzero" class="Primitive">lzero</a><a id="2832" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="2834" href="Agda.Primitive.html#lsuc" class="Primitive">lsuc</a><a id="2838" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

To solve this problem we need:

  - Σ-type definition

  - Product type definition

  - Review the recursion principle, what exactly it consists of.
    Maybe this refresh our minds (see Pp. 42 HoTT-Book).

    <p class="equation">
    $$ \mathsf{rec}_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}
      : \prod\limits_{(C : U)} (\Pi_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C) \rightarrow
        \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C
    $$
    </p>

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Σ-type (sigma type) definition (see the definition without projections
[here](https://github.com/jonaprieto/hott-book/blob/master/other/prelim.agda#L20)):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3521" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81" class="Module">Σ-Def₁</a> <a id="3535" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="3544" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="3553" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3554" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3554" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="3556" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3556" class="Bound">b</a><a id="3557" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3559" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3560" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3560" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3562" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3564" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="3568" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3554" class="Bound">a</a><a id="3569" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3572" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3572" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="3574" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3576" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3560" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3578" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3580" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="3584" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3556" class="Bound">b</a><a id="3585" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3587" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3589" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="3593" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3594" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3554" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="3596" href="Agda.Primitive.html#_%E2%8A%94_" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3556" class="Bound">b</a><a id="3599" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3601" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="3611" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ._,_" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3._%2C_" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
    <a id="3631" class="Keyword">field</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₁" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3.proj%E2%82%81" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="3649" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3651" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3560" class="Bound">A</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₂" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3.proj%E2%82%82" class="Field">proj₂</a> <a id="3665" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3667" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3572" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="3669" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3.proj%E2%82%81" class="Field">proj₁</a>

  <a id="3678" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3683" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="3685" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="3692" class="Comment">-- _,_ : (proj₁ : A) → B proj₁ → Σ A B.</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Its recursor with a function $$g : \prod_{(x : A)} B(x)\rightarrow C$$
that we provide.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3846" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Σ-Rec₁" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Rec%E2%82%81" class="Module">Σ-Rec₁</a> <a id="3860" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3861" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3861" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="3863" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3863" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="3865" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3865" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3866" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3868" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3868" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3870" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3872" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="3876" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3861" class="Bound">i</a><a id="3877" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3879" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3879" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="3881" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3883" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3868" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3885" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3887" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="3891" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3863" class="Bound">j</a><a id="3892" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3894" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3894" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="3896" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3898" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="3902" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3865" class="Bound">k</a><a id="3903" class="Symbol">}</a>
             <a id="3918" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3919" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3919" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="3921" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3923" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3924" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3924" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3926" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3868" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3929" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3931" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3933" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3879" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="3935" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3924" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3937" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3939" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#3894" class="Bound">C</a><a id="3940" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3942" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="3951" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3956" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81" class="Module">Σ-Def₁</a> <a id="3963" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="3969" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3970" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="3972" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="3974" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3.proj%E2%82%81" class="Field">proj₁</a><a id="3979" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="3981" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3.proj%E2%82%82" class="Field">proj₂</a><a id="3986" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="3988" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3._%2C_" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a> <a id="3992" class="Symbol">)</a>

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the other hand, the product type is just a particular case of the sigma type
when the codomain is not dependent, as we can see next by omitting the argument
in `(λ _ → B)`.

Its recursor with a function $$g : A \rightarrow B \rightarrow C$$ that we provide.

### Exercise 1.3

<p class="exercise">
Derive the induction principle for products $$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$$,
using only the projections and the propositional uniqueness principle
$$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$.
Verify that the definitional equalities are valid.
</p>

To solve this problem, recall the uniqueness principle (Pp. 29. HoTT-Book)

- The **propositional uniqueness principle** says that
every element of $$A\times B$$ is equal to a pair.

<p class="equation">
  $$ \mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}
     : \prod_{(x : A \times B)} ((\mathsf{proj}_{1}(x) , \mathsf{proj}_{2}(x))
       \equiv_{A\times B} x).
  $$
</p>

Product type definition using `data`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5564" class="Comment">-- this would be trivial in agda due to definitional η for records</a>
<a id="5631" class="Comment">-- so Capriotti defined a product type without η:</a>
<a id="5681" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₂" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Def%E2%82%82" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="5695" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="5704" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="×-Def₂._×_" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Def%E2%82%82._%C3%97_" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a> <a id="5713" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5714" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5714" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5716" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5716" class="Bound">j</a><a id="5717" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5719" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5719" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5721" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5723" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="5727" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5714" class="Bound">i</a><a id="5728" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5730" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5730" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="5732" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5734" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="5738" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5716" class="Bound">j</a><a id="5739" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5741" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5743" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="5747" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5748" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5714" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5750" href="Agda.Primitive.html#_%E2%8A%94_" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5752" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5716" class="Bound">j</a><a id="5753" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5755" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="×-Def₂._×_._,_" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Def%E2%82%82._%C3%97_._%2C_" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a> <a id="5769" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5771" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5719" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5773" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5775" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5730" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="5777" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5779" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5719" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5781" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Def%E2%82%82._%C3%97_" class="Datatype Operator">×</a> <a id="5783" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#5730" class="Bound">B</a>

  <a id="×-Fun₂.pair=" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Fun%E2%82%82.pair%3D" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="6483" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6485" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6487" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6488" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6488" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6490" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6492" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6494" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="6497" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6499" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6500" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6500" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6502" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6502" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="6504" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6506" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6488" class="Bound">A</a><a id="6507" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6509" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6510" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6510" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6512" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6512" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="6514" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6516" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6490" class="Bound">B</a><a id="6517" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="6527" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6529" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6500" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6531" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="6533" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6502" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="6535" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6537" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6510" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="6541" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6512" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="6543" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6545" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6546" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6500" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6548" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Def%E2%82%82._%C3%97_._%2C_" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6550" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6510" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6551" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6553" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="6555" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6556" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6502" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="6558" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Def%E2%82%82._%C3%97_._%2C_" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6560" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#6512" class="Bound">z</a><a id="6561" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="6565" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Fun%E2%82%82.pair%3D" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="6571" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_.refl" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="6576" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_.refl" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="6581" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6583" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_.refl" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The induction principle for the product type:

<p class="equation">
$$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B} : \prod\limits_{C : A \times B \to \mathcal{U}}
  \left( \prod\limits_{x:A}\ \prod\limits_{y:B}\ \,C( (x,y) ) \right)
  \to \prod\limits_{x:A \times B}\ \,C(x)
$$
</p>

          <a id="7270" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7272" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Ind%E2%82%82.ind" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="7276" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7169" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="7278" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7201" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="7280" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7281" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7283" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Def%E2%82%82._%C3%97_._%2C_" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7253" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7286" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7288" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="7290" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7201" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="7292" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7294" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7253" class="Bound">y</a>
  <a id="7298" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Ind%E2%82%82.ind-%CE%B2" class="Function">ind-β</a> <a id="7304" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7304" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="7306" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7306" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="7308" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7308" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7310" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#7310" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7312" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7314" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_.refl" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<p class="exercise">
Generalize $$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$ to Σ-types, and do the same for
$$\Sigma$$-types, i.e. show induction and verify the definitional equality
is valid.
</p>

Σ-type definition using `data`:

### Exercise 1.4

<div class="exercise">
Assuming as given only the <em>iterator</em> for natural numbers
<p class="equation">
$$\mathsf{ite} : \prod\limits_{C:\mathcal{U}} C \to (C \to C) \to \mathbb{N} \to C $$
</p>
with the defining equations
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,0)               &\equiv c_0, \\
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,\mathsf{suc}(n)) &\equiv c_s(\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,n)),
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
derive a function having the type of the recursor $$\mathsf{rec}$$.
Show that the defining equations of the recursor hold propositionally for this
function, using the induction principle for $$\mathbb{N}$$.
</div>

To solve this problem, let us define the recursor and also the induction principle
for natural numbers. (See more details about these functions in
[Induction on Natural Numbers]({% post_url 2018-02-12-induction-on-natural-numbers %})).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9375" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Def" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%E2%84%95-Def" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="9388" class="Keyword">where</a>

       <a id="9718" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9720" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="9723" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9724" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#9724" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="9726" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9728" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%E2%84%95-Def.%E2%84%95" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="9729" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9731" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9733" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#9641" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9735" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#9724" class="Bound">n</a><a id="9736" class="Symbol">)</a>

Now, we define the iterator following the equations above:

Then, we now can define the recursor using this `ite` by iterating over the type
`ℕ × C` (*reloading recursion*?).


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10228" class="Comment">-- recursor</a>

           <a id="10481" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#10354" class="Bound">n</a><a id="10482" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, we need to establish the propositional equality between these two
definitions of recursor, i.e, between `rec` and `rec₂`. Let's use
induction to prove that.

      <a id="11372" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#11308" class="Function">u</a> <a id="11374" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11376" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%C3%97-Fun%E2%82%82.ap-proj%E2%82%82" class="Function">ap-proj₂</a>  <a id="11386" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11387" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="11389" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%E2%84%95-Def.%E2%84%95" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="11392" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11394" class="Argument">B</a> <a id="11396" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11398" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#11011" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11399" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11401" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#ex1-4.proof" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="11408" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#11011" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#11013" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#11016" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#11024" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11417" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Exercise 1.5

<div class="exercise">

Show that if we define

  $$A+B :\equiv \sum\limits_{(x : \mathbbbold{2})} \mathsf{rec}_{\mathbbbold{2}} (\mathcal{U}, A , B, x),$$

then we can give a definition of $$\ind\limits_{A + B}$$ for which the
definitional equalities holds.

</div>

To solve this problem, let us introduce the $$\mathcal{2}$$ type, that is, the
type with two constructors also called **Bool**. The constructors are also called
false and true respectively.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11922" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="11936" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="11945" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A" class="Datatype">𝟚</a> <a id="11952" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11954" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="11958" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟘" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A.%F0%9D%9F%98" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="11970" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11972" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟙" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A.%F0%9D%9F%99" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="11980" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11982" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

  <a id="12641" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12641" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12643" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Def%E2%82%81._%2B_" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="12645" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12645" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="12647" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12649" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="12651" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A" class="Datatype">𝟚</a> <a id="12653" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12654" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Rec%E2%82%81.rec" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="12658" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12641" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12660" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12645" class="Bound">B</a><a id="12661" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12663" class="Comment">-- if it&#39;s 𝟘 return A otherwise returns B</a>

  <a id="12708" class="Comment">-- the tradional constructors</a>
  <a id="+-Def₁.inl" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Def%E2%82%81.inl" class="Function">inl</a> <a id="12744" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12746" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12748" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12749" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12749" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12750" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12752" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12752" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12754" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12754" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="12756" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12758" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="12762" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12749" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12763" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12765" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12767" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12752" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12769" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12771" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12752" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12773" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Def%E2%82%81._%2B_" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="12775" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#12754" class="Bound">B</a>

Now, let's try to define the recursor for this coproduct, and later,
we'll try the dependent version of it to complete the exercise.

  <a id="13220" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Rec%E2%82%81.rec" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13224" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#13224" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13226" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#13226" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13228" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A.%F0%9D%9F%99" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13231" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%CE%A3-Def%E2%82%81.%CE%A3._%2C_" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13233" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#13233" class="Bound">b</a><a id="13234" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13236" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13238" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#13226" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13240" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#13233" class="Bound">b</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Notice how the recursor of the coproduct matches with the elimination
rule of the disjunction conective also called *case analysis*. That's follows from the
[**propositions-as-types**](https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/propositions+as+types).

![path](/assets/latexit-images/disj-elimination.png)

Finally, the induction principle for the coproduct:

  <a id="13678" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13683" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="13690" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13696" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13697" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A.%F0%9D%9F%98" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="13698" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13699" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A.%F0%9D%9F%99" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="13700" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13701" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%9A-Def%E2%82%81.%F0%9D%9F%9A" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="13702" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="14300" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Ind%E2%82%81.ind-%CE%B2%E2%82%82" class="Function">ind-β₂</a> <a id="14307" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#14307" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14309" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#14309" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14311" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#14311" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14313" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14315" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_.refl" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Chapter 3

### Exercise 3.1

<div class="exercise">
Prove that if $$A\simeq B$$ and $$A$$ is a set, then so is $$B$$.
</div>
To solve this problem, let us recall a few things:

- The *set* definition in HoTT:

A type $$A$$ is a **set** if for all $$x, y : A$$ and
all $$p, q : x \equiv y$$, we have $$ p \equiv q$$. In a proposition
we have

$$
\mathsf{isSet}(A) :\equiv \prod\limits_{(x,y : A)}\prod\limits_{(p,q : x \equiv y)} (p \equiv q).
$$

- The type for equivalence from $$A$$ to $$B$$

$$
  (A \simeq B) :\equiv \sum\limits_{f : A \to B} \mathsf{isequiv}(f),
$$

where

$$
\mathsf{isequiv(f)} :\equiv
  \left (\sum\limits_{g : B \to A} (f \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{B})\right) \times
  \left (\sum\limits_{h : B \to A} (h \circ f \sim \mathsf{id}_{A})\right)
$$

- The homotopy concept:

Let $$f , g : \prod\limits_{(x:A)} P(x)$$ be two sections of a
type family $$P : A \to \mathcal{U}$$. A **homotopy** from $$f$$ to $$g$$
is a dependent function of type

$$
(f \sim g) :\equiv \prod\limits_{x : A} (f(x) \equiv g(x)).
$$

<div class="proof" id="proof-3.1">
Sketch of the proof.<br/>
Let be $$x,y : B$$ and $$p : x \equiv_{B} y$$ and $$q : x \equiv_{B} y$$.
We need to prove $$ p \equiv q$$.<br/>
Since $$A\simeq B$$ then there is a function $$f : A \to B$$ and some
$$g : B \to A$$ such that $$f \circ g \sim id_{B}$$.
Using this function $$g$$ over the path $$p$$ we get
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} p : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.
We do the same but this time over the path $$q$$, that is,
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} q : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.
Because of $$A$$ is a set, we have a new path called
$$m :\mathsf{ap}_{g} p \equiv_{gx \equiv_{A} gy} \mathsf{ap}_{g} q$$. <br/>

Now, an action over this path $$m$$
using the function $$\mathsf{ap}_{f} : x \equiv_{A} y \to f x \equiv_{B} f y$$
will give us

<p class="equation">
$$
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m :
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q).
$$
</p>
By the lemmas in Chapter 2, we do the following reasoning:

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q) &=
  \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} q\\
  &=\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{id}_{B}} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{id}_{B}} q\\
  &= p \equiv q.
\end{align*}
$$<br/>
</p>
Then, we have the inhabitant, $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m : p \equiv q$$.
</div>

Now, let's verify this in Agda.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="16779" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="sets" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#sets" class="Module">sets</a> <a id="16791" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="sets.isSet" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#sets.isSet" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="16806" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16808" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="16810" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16811" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16811" class="Bound">i</a><a id="16812" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16814" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16815" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16815" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16817" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16819" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="16823" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16811" class="Bound">i</a><a id="16824" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16826" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16828" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="16832" class="Symbol">_</a>
  <a id="16836" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#sets.isSet" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="16842" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16842" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16844" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16846" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16847" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16847" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16849" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16849" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="16851" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16853" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16842" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16854" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16856" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16858" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16859" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16859" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16861" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16863" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16849" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16868" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16870" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16872" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16873" href="{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16849" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16882" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16884" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16886" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16859" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16888" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#_%E2%89%A1_" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="16890" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#16873" class="Bound">q</a>

### Exercise 3.2

<div class="exercise">
Prove that if $$A$$ and $$B$$ are sets, then so is $$A+B$$.
</div>

To solve this exercise, we should take a look of some results from Chapter 2,
Section 2.12. But first let's define the empty type:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17169" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟘-Def" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%98-Def" class="Module">𝟘-Def</a> <a id="17182" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="17190" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="𝟘-Def.𝟘" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%98-Def.%F0%9D%9F%98" class="Datatype">𝟘</a> <a id="17197" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17199" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="17203" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="17210" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟘-Rec" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%98-Rec" class="Module">𝟘-Rec</a> <a id="17223" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="17231" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="17236" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%98-Def" class="Module">𝟘-Def</a>
  <a id="𝟘-Rec.rec" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%98-Rec.rec" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="17248" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17250" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17251" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#17251" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="17253" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17255" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="17258" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17260" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17262" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%98-Def.%F0%9D%9F%98" class="Datatype">𝟘</a> <a id="17264" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17266" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#17251" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="17270" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%98-Rec.rec" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="17274" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17276" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="17278" class="Symbol">()</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<div class="proof" id="proof-3.2">
Sketch of the Proof.<br/>

Let be $$x, y : A + B$$, and paths $$p : x \equiv y$$, $$q : x \equiv
y$$. Let's get a path $$p \equiv q$$.  We proceed by case analysis. If
$$x :\equiv \mathsf{inl} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$$, for
some $$a, b : A$$ then $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p : a
\equiv_{A} b$$ and $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q : a \equiv_{A}
b$$.

Since $$A$$ is a set, there is a path between these last two terms,
this is, $$m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p \equiv
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q$$.  Now, an action over this path
$$m$$ using the $$\mathsf{inl}$$ function give us:
$$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}} m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q)$$.<br/>

We conclude by Lemmas in Chapter 2, that $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
m : p \equiv q$$ since $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv p$$.<br/> Following the
same reasoning, we prove the case $$x :\equiv \mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y
:\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$.  For the latest cases, $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inl} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$ and $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$$, we use the
encode-decode method to derive a proof term for 𝟘 from
$$p$$ and $$q$$. Then, we may conclude anything we wish, that is, $$p
\equiv q$$.  </div>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="18728" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Def₂" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Def%E2%82%82" class="Module">+-Def₂</a> <a id="18742" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="+-Def₂._+_.inl" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Def%E2%82%82._%2B_.inl" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="18793" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18795" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="18797" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18798" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18798" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18800" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18802" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="18805" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18807" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18810" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18810" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18814" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="18817" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18819" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18821" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18810" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18823" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Def%E2%82%82._%2B_" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="18825" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18798" class="Bound">B</a>
    <a id="+-Def₂._+_.inr" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Def%E2%82%82._%2B_.inr" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="18835" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18837" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="18839" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18840" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18840" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18842" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18844" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="18847" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18849" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18852" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18852" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18854" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18856" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="18859" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18861" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18863" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18840" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18865" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Def%E2%82%82._%2B_" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="18867" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18852" class="Bound">B</a>

  <a id="18893" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="18898" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Def%E2%82%82" class="Module">+-Def₂</a>

  <a id="18920" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="18925" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%F0%9D%9F%98-Rec" class="Module">𝟘-Rec</a>

  <a id="+-Fun₂.code" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#%2B-Fun%E2%82%82.code" class="Function">code</a> <a id="18939" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18941" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18942" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18942" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18944" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-HoTT-book.md %}{% raw %}#18944" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18946" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18948" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="18951" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="19262" class="Comment">-- ind : {A B : Set}</a>
  <a id="19285" class="Comment">--     → (C : A + B → Set)</a>
  <a id="19314" class="Comment">--     → ((x : A) → C (inl x))</a>
  <a id="19347" class="Comment">--     → ((x : B) → C (inr x))</a>
  <a id="19380" class="Comment">--     → (x : A + B) → C x</a>
  <a id="19409" class="Comment">-- ind C f g c x = {!   !}</a>

### Exercise 3.3

<div class="exercise">
Prove that if $$ A $$ is a set and $$B : A \to \mathcal{U}$$
is a type family such that $$B(x)$$ is a set for all
$$x : A$$, then $$\Sigma\limits_{(x:A)}\ B(x)$$ is a set.
</div>

### Exercise 3.4

<div class="exercise">
Show that $$A$$ is a mere proposition if and only
if $$A\to A$$ is contractible.
</div>

* Univalent Foundations Program, T. (2013). Homotopy Type Theory: Univalent Foundations of Mathematics. Institute for Advanced Study.

* [Capriotti's hott-exercises](https://github.com/pcapriotti/hott-exercises).

* [Capriotti's agda-base](https://github.com/pcapriotti/agda-base/)
